(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});
[
['adRendered', onRequiredDomEvent],
['beforeunload', onRequiredDomEvent],
['load', function() { setTimeout(onRequiredDomEvent, deferLoadTime); }]
].forEach(function(event) {
window.addEventListener(event[0], event[1], { once: true });
});

(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});
[
['adRendered', onRequiredDomEvent],
['beforeunload', onRequiredDomEvent],
['load', function() { setTimeout(onRequiredDomEvent, deferLoadTime); }]
].forEach(function(event) {
window.addEventListener(event[0], event[1], { once: true });
});

(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});

<div id="health-a-to-z-container_1-0" class="comp health-a-to-z-container mntl-block"><h3 id="health-a-to-z-container__title_1-0" class="comp health-a-to-z-container__title mntl-text-block healthHomeTemplate__section-heading">HEALTH A-Z</h3>
<div id="health-a-to-z_1-0" class="comp health-a-to-z mntl-block"><div id="alphabetical-nav_1-0" class="comp alphabetical-nav pagination" data-tracking-container="true"> <h3 class="section-title">Find a topic by its first letter:</h3>
<ol class="alphabetical-nav-list">

(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});
[
['adRendered', onRequiredDomEvent],
['beforeunload', onRequiredDomEvent],
['load', function() { setTimeout(onRequiredDomEvent, deferLoadTime); }]
].forEach(function(event) {
window.addEventListener(event[0], event[1], { once: true });
});
})(Mntl.fnUtilities || {}, Mntl.CMP);window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});
[
['adRendered', onRequiredDomEvent],
['beforeunload', onRequiredDomEvent],
['load', function() { setTimeout(onRequiredDomEvent, deferLoadTime); }]
].forEach(function(event) {
window.addEventListener(event[0], event[1], { once: true });
});
})(Mntl.fnUtilities || {}, Mntl.CMP);window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

<div id="latest-news_1-0" class="comp latest-news mntl-block"><h2 id="latest-news__title_1-0" class="comp latest-news__title mntl-text-block">News and Trending</h2>
<div id="mntl-document-card-list_1-0" class="comp mntl-document-card-list mntl-card-list mntl-block" data-chunk="36"><a id="mntl-card-list-items_1-0" class="comp mntl-card-list-items mntl-document-card mntl-card card card--no-image" data-doc-id="8621602" data-tax-levels="" href="https://www.verywellhealth.com/new-high-blood-pressure-drug-tryvio-8621602" data-ordinal="1">
<div class="card__content ">
<div class="card__header"></div>
<span class="card__title"><span class="card__title-text ">FDA Approves the First New Type of High Blood Pressure Drug In Decades</span></span>
<div id="card__byline-block_2-0" class="comp card__byline-block mntl-block"><div id="card__byline_2-0" class="comp card__byline mntl-block mntl-card__byline" data-byline="By Stephanie Brown"></div>

(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});
[
['adRendered', onRequiredDomEvent],
['beforeunload', onRequiredDomEvent],
['load', function() { setTimeout(onRequiredDomEvent, deferLoadTime); }]
].forEach(function(event) {
window.addEventListener(event[0], event[1], { once: true });
});

<div id="mntl-block_1-0" class="comp mntl-block healthHomeTemplate__row healthHomeTemplate__row--primary"><section id="spotlight-home_1-0" class="comp spotlight-home mntl-block" data-tracking-container="true"><div id="spotlight-home__top_1-0" class="comp spotlight-home__top mntl-block"><a id="spotlight-home__featured_1-0" class="comp spotlight-home__featured spotlight-home__card block block block--large " rel="" data-doc-id="" href="https://www.verywellhealth.com/which-providers-prescribe-glps-weight-loss-8609302">

<div id="our-promise_1-1" class="comp our-promise mntl-block" data-tracking-container="true"><div id="our-promise__sidebar_1-1" class="comp our-promise__sidebar mntl-block"><div id="our-promise__headline_1-1" class="comp our-promise__headline mntl-text-block">Our content is here to help you make the best choices for your health.</div>
